  svg: '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" fill="none" viewBox="0 0 24 24" stroke-width="1.5" stroke="currentColor" class="size-6"> <path stroke-linecap="round" stroke-linejoin="round" d="M21 11.25v8.25a1.5 1.5 0 0 1-1.5 1.5H5.25a1.5 1.5 0 0 1-1.5-1.5v-8.25M12 4.875A2.625 2.625 0 1 0 9.375 7.5H12m0-2.625V7.5m0-2.625A2.625 2.625 0 1 1 14.625 7.5H12m0 0V21m-8.625-9.75h18c.621 0 1.125-.504 1.125-1.125v-1.5c0-.621-.504-1.125-1.125-1.125h-18c-.621 0-1.125.504-1.125 1.125v1.5c0 .621.504 1.125 1.125 1.125Z" /></svg>',  //Be sure there are no line breaks in the svg value    
   },    
  {
      text: '[unlock-icon]',  
   svg: '<svg xmlns="http://www.w3.org/2000/svg" viewBox="0 0 24 24" fill="currentColor" class="size-6">  <path d="M18 1.5c2.9 0 5.25 2.35 5.25 5.25v3.75a.75.75 0 0 1-1.5 0V6.75a3.75 3.75 0 1 0-7.5 0v3a3 3 0 0 1 3 3v6.75a3 3 0 0 1-3 3H3.75a3 3 0 0 1-3-3v-6.75a3 3 0 0 1 3-3h9v-3c0-2.9 2.35-5.25 5.25-5.25Z" /></svg>',  //Be sure there are no line breaks in the svg value    
   },       
    
  /*Icon Template end*/
  ];
 
     
  // Function to replace text with Icon
  function replaceAccordionTitleWithIcon() {
    let elements = document.querySelectorAll(".accordion-item button *");
    let classes = 'accordion-icon';

    for (let element of elements) {
      if (element.childNodes.length === 1 && element.childNodes[0].nodeType === 3) {
        let textNode = element.childNodes[0];
        let replacedText = textNode.nodeValue;

        for (let replacement of accordionIcons) {
          if (!replacedText.includes(replacement.text)) continue;
          replacedText = replacedText.replace(replacement.text, replacement.svg);
          let span = document.createElement("span");
          span.innerHTML = replacedText;
          if (classes) span.classList = classes;
          element.replaceChild(span, textNode);
        }
      }
    }
  }

  setTimeout(replaceAccordionTitleWithIcon, 0);
  window.addEventListener('load', replaceAccordionTitleWithIcon)
</script>

<!-- ==========================
  Deferred Table of Contents Initialisation
  Purpose:
    Prevents console errors ("Cannot read properties of null (reading 'innerHTML')")
    caused when toc.js executes before the article DOM has fully rendered.
  Added: 05 Nov 2025 — Fixes jQuery.Deferred console warnings on Squarespace 7.0.
  Context:
    Squarespace hydrates content asynchronously, so toc.js sometimes fires too early.
  Strategy:
    Wait for DOMContentLoaded, confirm toc.js is loaded, then run generateToc()
    after 1.5s to ensure article elements exist.
  ========================== -->
<script>
document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {
  // Ensure toc.js has loaded successfully and exposes generateToc()
  if (typeof window.generateToc === "function") {
    setTimeout(function() {
      try {
        window.generateToc();
        console.log("Deferred TOC: Successfully initialised (1.5s delay).");
      } catch (err) {
        console.warn("Deferred TOC: Skipped -", err.message);
      }
    }, 1500); // Delay ensures Squarespace article DOM exists
  } else {
    console.log("Deferred TOC: generateToc() not detected, skipping.");
  }
});
</script>
<!-- ========================== END Deferred TOC Initialisation ========================== -->

<!-- Remove Squarespace LocalBusiness/Organization schema -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function () {
    const ldScripts = document.querySelectorAll('script[type="application/ld+json"]');
    ldScripts.forEach((script) => {
      try {
        const json = JSON.parse(script.innerText);
        if (
          json["@type"] === "LocalBusiness" ||
          json["@type"] === "Organization" ||
          (Array.isArray(json) && json.some(item => item["@type"] === "LocalBusiness" || item["@type"] === "Organization"))
        ) {
          script.remove(); // Remove only broken Squarespace schema
        }
      } catch (e) {}
    });
  });
</script>

<!-- Estimated Reading Time Blog Posts -->
<script>

$(function () {

    var txt = $("article")[0].textContent,

    wordCount = txt.replace( /[^\w ]/g, "" ).split( /\s+/ ).length;

    var readingTimeInMinutes = Math.floor(wordCount / 228) + 1;

    var readingTimeAsString = readingTimeInMinutes + " min";

    $('article .reading-time').html(readingTimeAsString);

});

</script>

 Suppress Squarespace Microdata — v1.7 HARD STRIP (Nov 2025)
 Purpose: Fully remove Squarespace duplicate microdata before crawl
 =============================== -->
<script>
(function(){
  const killAttrs = el=>{
    ['itemtype','itemprop','itemscope','itemid'].forEach(a=>el.removeAttribute(a));
  };
  const purge = ()=>{
    document.querySelectorAll('[itemscope],[itemtype],[itemprop],[itemid]').forEach(killAttrs);
  };
  // run early, then twice more post-hydration
  purge();
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', purge);
  window.addEventListener('load', ()=>setTimeout(purge, 800));
  // catch dynamic SSR hydration loops every 2 s for 6 s total
  let t=0; const interval=setInterval(()=>{purge(); if(++t>3) clearInterval(interval);},2000);
})();
</script>

<!-- Block Squarespace-injected Product schemas only -->
<script>
(function () {
  const removeProductSchema = () => {
    const scripts = document.querySelectorAll('script[type="application/ld+json"]');

    scripts.forEach((script) => {
      try {
        const json = JSON.parse(script.textContent);

        if (
          json['@type'] === 'Product' ||
          (Array.isArray(json['@type']) && json['@type'].includes('Product'))
        ) {
          // Optional safety: only remove if there's no review/aggregateRating
          const hasReviewData = json.review || json.aggregateRating;
          if (!hasReviewData) {
            script.remove();
          }
        }
      } catch (e) {
        // Ignore malformed scripts
      }
    });
  };

  // Run once on DOM ready
  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", removeProductSchema);

  // Run continuously for any future injections
  const observer = new MutationObserver(() => {
    removeProductSchema();
  });

  observer.observe(document.body, {
    childList: true,
    subtree: true
  });
})();
</script>

<!-- BACK TO TOP BUTTON ANIMATION (7.0 & 7.1) -->
<script>
  var scrolled = 400; $(window).scroll(function() {
    if ( $(window).scrollTop() > scrolled ) {
      $('a.btt').fadeIn('slow');
    } else {
      $('a.btt').fadeOut('slow');
    }
  });

    $('html, body').animate({ scrollTop: 0 }, 700);

  });

<!--Mega Menu 7.0 -->
<script>
$(document).ready(function () {
    // Define the hover timeout duration in milliseconds
    var hoverTimeoutDuration = 3000; // Example: 3000ms (3 seconds)

    $('.Header-nav-folder-title[href^="/mega-"]').each(function () {
        var e = $(this).attr("href").slice(6);
        $(this).parent().addClass("mega-menu");
        var a = $(this).closest("header.Header");
        a.append("<div id=" + e + ' class="mega-menu-item"></div>');
        $("#" + e).load("/mega-menu-pages #mega-page-" + e, function () {
            window.Squarespace.initializeLayoutBlocks(Y, Y.one("#" + e));
            var imgs = document.querySelectorAll(".mega-menu-item img[data-src]");
            for (var n = 0; n < imgs.length; n++) {
                ImageLoader.load(imgs[n], { load: true, fill: true });
                imgs[n].parentNode.className += " loaded";
            }
        });
        var hoverTimeout;
        // Function to start hover timeout
        function startHoverTimeout() {
            clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
            hoverTimeout = setTimeout(function () {
                removeHoverFromAll();
            }, hoverTimeoutDuration);
        }
        // Function to remove hover from all mega menus
        function removeHoverFromAll() {
            $('.mega-menu-item').removeClass('hover');
            $('.mega-menu').removeClass('hover');
        }
        // Handle hover on the link's parent
        $(this).parent().hover(
            function () {
                removeHoverFromAll(); // Remove hover from all other mega menus
                a.find("#" + e).addClass("hover");
                clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
                // Monitor mouse movement to reset hover timeout
                $(document).on("mousemove.megaMenu", function () {
                    clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
                    startHoverTimeout();
                });
            },
            function () {
                startHoverTimeout();
                $(document).off("mousemove.megaMenu");
            }
        );
        // Handle hover on the mega menu content
        $("#" + e).hover(
            function () {
                a.find("#" + e).addClass("hover");
                clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);

                // Monitor mouse movement to reset hover timeout
                $(document).on("mousemove.megaMenuContent", function () {
                    clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
                    startHoverTimeout();
                });
            },
            function () {
                startHoverTimeout();
                $(document).off("mousemove.megaMenuContent");
            }
        );
        // Detect hover on anything outside the mega menu or its link
        $("body").on("mouseenter", "*", function (event) {
            var target = $(event.target);
            if (!target.closest(".mega-menu, .mega-menu-item").length) {
                removeHoverFromAll();
                clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
            }
        });
        // Remove hover on scroll
        $(window).on("scroll.megaMenu", function () {
            removeHoverFromAll();
            clearTimeout(hoverTimeout);
        });
    });
});
</script>
<!--end Mega Menu 7.0 -->


<!-- SLIDESHOW HEIGHT ON MOBILE - by beatrizcaraballo.com -->
<script>
  setTimeout(function() {
    var $galleryContainer = $('.sqs-gallery-design-stacked');
    var $slides = $galleryContainer.find('.slide');

    function setGalleryHeight() {
      var maxHeight = 0;

      $slides.each(function() {
        var slideHeight = $(this).outerHeight();
        maxHeight = Math.max(maxHeight, slideHeight);
      });

      $galleryContainer.css('height', maxHeight);
    }

    setGalleryHeight();

    $(window).on('resize', function() {
      setGalleryHeight();
    });
  }, 2000);
</script>

    });

<!-- Add BlueSky Icon -->
<script>
  document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', () => {
    function replaceBskyIcons() {
      const symbolContainer = document.querySelector('[data-usage="social-icons-svg"]');
      if (symbolContainer && !document.getElementById('wm-bsky')) {
        const symbolDef = `<symbol id="wm-bsky" viewBox="0 0 64 64">
  <path d="M22.1 20.0406C26.1091 23.001 30.4455 28.7618 32 31.9623V40.4434C32 40.2834 32.0818 40.4434 32.2455 40.9235C33.0636 43.3238 36.2545 52.6051 43.7 45.1641C47.5455 41.2435 45.7455 37.323 38.7091 36.2029C42.7182 36.8429 47.3 35.7228 48.5273 31.4022C49.3455 30.122 50 22.601 50 21.4808C50 16.2801 45.3364 17.8803 41.9 20.0406L41.9328 20.02Z"></path>
</symbol>`;
        symbolContainer.insertAdjacentHTML('beforeend', symbolDef);
      }

      // Find all Bluesky icons and replace their content
      const bskyHeaderLinks = document.querySelectorAll('.icon[href*="https://bsky.app"], .sqs-svg-icon--wrapper[href*="https://bsky.app"]');
      console.log(bskyHeaderLinks)
      bskyHeaderLinks.forEach(link => {
        console.log('replace', link)
        link.innerHTML = '<svg viewBox="23 23 64 64"><use xlink:href="#wm-bsky" width="110" height="110"></use></svg>';
      });
    }
    replaceBskyIcons();
  })
</script>

<script type="module">
  import('https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/alanranger/alanranger-reviews@main/reviews-1.js')
    .then(({ default: reviews }) => {
      const container = document.getElementById('testimonial-widget');
      if (!container) return;

      const MAX_DISPLAY = 5;

      const filtered = reviews
        .filter(r => r.rating >= 4) // Only 4-star and 5-star
        .sort((a, b) => new Date(b.date) - new Date(a.date)) // Most recent first
        .slice(0, MAX_DISPLAY);

      container.innerHTML = '';

      filtered.forEach(r => {
        const div = document.createElement('div');
        div.className = 'testimonial';
        div.innerHTML = `
          <p><strong>${r.reviewer}</strong> <span style="color: green">(${r.source})</span></p>
          <p><em>${r.title}</em></p>
          <p>${r.body}</p>
          <p><strong>Event:</strong> <span style="color: orange">${r.event}</span> | <strong>Rating:</strong> ${'⭐'.repeat(r.rating)}</p>
          <hr/>
        `;
        container.appendChild(div);
      });
    });
</script>

<!-- Accordion Icons Reliability Fix — 2025-11-05 (body-safe version) -->
<script>
(function(){
  function replaceAccordionIcons(){
    var icons = window.accordionIcons || [];
    if(!icons.length) return;
    var roots = document.querySelectorAll(
      '.sqs-block-accordion, .accordion-block, .accordion, .accordion-item'
    );
    if(!roots.length) return;

    roots.forEach(function(root){
      if(root.__iconsApplied) return;
      var walker = document.createTreeWalker(root, NodeFilter.SHOW_TEXT, {
        acceptNode:function(node){
          if(!node.nodeValue || !node.nodeValue.trim()) return NodeFilter.FILTER_REJECT;
          if(node.parentElement && node.parentElement.classList.contains('accordion-icon'))
            return NodeFilter.FILTER_REJECT;
          return /\[[a-z0-9\-]+-icon\]/i.test(node.nodeValue)
            ? NodeFilter.FILTER_ACCEPT
            : NodeFilter.FILTER_REJECT;
        }
      });
      var toProcess=[];
      while(walker.nextNode()) toProcess.push(walker.currentNode);

      toProcess.forEach(function(textNode){
        var original=textNode.nodeValue, replaced=original;
        for(var i=0;i<icons.length;i++){
          var key=icons[i].text, svg=icons[i].svg;
          if(replaced.indexOf(key)!==-1){
            replaced=replaced.split(key).join(svg);
          }
        }
        if(replaced!==original){
          var span=document.createElement('span');
          span.className='accordion-icon';
          span.innerHTML=replaced;
          textNode.parentNode.replaceChild(span,textNode);
        }
      });
      root.__iconsApplied=true;
    });
  }

  function safeRun(){
    try{ replaceAccordionIcons(); }catch(e){} 
  }

  function startWhenReady(){
    if(!document.body){ setTimeout(startWhenReady, 150); return; }
    safeRun();
    window.addEventListener('load', safeRun);
    [500,1200,2500,4000].forEach(function(t){ setTimeout(safeRun,t); });

    // MutationObserver (now guaranteed valid)
    try{
      var mo=new MutationObserver(function(muts){
        for(var i=0;i<muts.length;i++){
          if(muts[i].addedNodes && muts[i].addedNodes.length){ safeRun(); break; }
        }
      });
      mo.observe(document.body,{childList:true,subtree:true});
    }catch(e){}
  }

  startWhenReady();
})();
</script>

  document.addEventListener("DOMContentLoaded", function() {

          gtag('event', 'cta_click', {
            'event_category': 'CTA',
            'event_label': link.getAttribute("data-cta"),
            'value': 1
          });
        }
      });
    });
  });
</script>
